<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:реактор.html>реа́ктор</a> (11867)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реактор.html>реа́ктор</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">reáktor</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реактор.html>реа́ктора</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реактор.html>реа́кторы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реактор.html>реа́кторов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>reactor <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a device which uses atomic energy to produce heat</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реализм.html>реали́зм</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">realízm</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реализм.html>реали́зма</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реализовать.html>реализова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">realizovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:реализовать.html>реализова́ть</a></strong></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реализовывать.html>реализо́вывать</a></b>)

<li>to sell, to convert into cash</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реализовать.html>реализова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">realizovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:реализовывать.html>реализо́вывать</a> (28454)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реализовать.html>реализова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">realizovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реализовывать.html>реализо́вывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">realizóvyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реализовать.html>реализова́ть</a></b>)
</p>

<li>to sell, to realize</li></ol>

***реально.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:реальный.html>реально</a> (5784)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реальный.html>реа́льный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">reálʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реальный.html>реа́льно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">reálʹno</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-реа́льно" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)реа́льнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-реа́льно" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)реа́льней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>really, in reality</li>
<li>objectively</li>
<li>specifically, factually</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реальный.html>реа́льно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">reálʹno</span>)
</p>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ре.html>ре</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:аль.html>а́ль</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:реанимация.html>реанима́ция</a> (15100)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реанимация.html>реанима́ция</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">reanimácija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реанимация.html>реанима́ции</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реанимация.html>реанима́ции</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реанимация.html>реанима́ций</a></b>)

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> resuscitation</li>

***ребенок.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>ребёнок</a> (174)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">робя</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">robja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, diminitive of <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">робъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">robŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">slave</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*orbę</i>. Compare with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">па́робок</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">párobok</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lad</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>. The relationship with "slave" could arise from the meaning "orphan" because orphans carried out the hard work in the household.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>ребёнок</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rebjónok</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>ребёнка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>де́ти</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>ребя́та</a><sup>*</sup></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>дете́й</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>ребя́т</a><sup>*</sup></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:детский.html>де́тский</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребеночек.html>ребёночек</a></b>) <span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">(</span></span><span class="ib-content"><span class="qualifier-content">* Use the second plural with the meaning "friends!", "fellows!", "guys!", "comrades!".</span></span><span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">)</span></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">plural <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>де́ти</a></span>, less commonly <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>ребя́та</a></span></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> child, kid, baby: children, kids, babies
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дитя.html>дитя́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ditjá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">plural only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">plural <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>ребя́та</a></span></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> guys, fellows, friends, comrades</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The singular form can only refer to "child"/"baby" sense.</li>
<li>The plural form <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>ребя́та</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rebjáta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> can mean "guys", "friends", etc.</li>
<li>For the plural form "children" <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>де́ти</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">déti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is the preferred word but <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>ребя́та</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rebjáta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is also used.</li>
<li>The suppletive plural form <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>де́ти</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">déti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is originally a plural form of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дитя.html>дитя́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ditjá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ре.html>ре</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>бё<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>нок</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 3*a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка). <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>Также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>значе́нии</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:множественный.html>мно́жественного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:число.html>числа</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:использоваться.html>испо́льзоваться</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>ребя́та</a></i>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-реб-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ёнок</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ребро.html>ребро́</a> (4258)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*rebrò</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребро.html>ребро́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rebró</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребро.html>ребра́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребро.html>рёбра</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребро.html>рёбер</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">anatomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> rib</li>
<li>edge, verge, arc</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> roentgenizdat; music illicitly reproduced on X-ray film</li></ol>

***ребус.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ребус.html>ре́бус</a> (29273)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребус.html>ре́бус</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rébus</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребус.html>ре́буса</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребус.html>ре́бусы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребус.html>ре́бусов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>rebus</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реверанс.html>ревера́нс</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">reveráns</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реверанс.html>ревера́нса</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реверанс.html>ревера́нсы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реверанс.html>ревера́нсов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>curtsey</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> servility</li></ol>

***реветь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:реветь.html>реве́ть</a> (4085)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Infinitive modified by analogy with 1sg. <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реветь.html>реву́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">revú</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">рюти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rjuti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*řuti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реветь.html>реве́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">revétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взреветь.html>взреве́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зареветь.html>зареве́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прореветь.html>прореве́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to roar, to bellow, to howl</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cry, to weep (loudly)</li></ol>

***ревизия.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ревизия.html>реви́зия</a> (14661)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">rewizja</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">revīsiō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">review</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; original meaning "census of the male population". From the time of Peter I.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ревизия.html>реви́зия</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">revízija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ревизия.html>реви́зии</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ревизия.html>реви́зии</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ревизия.html>реви́зий</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ревизио́нный</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>audit <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">independent review</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> inspection, examination</li>
<li>revision <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a theory or treaty</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> census of the male population <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">for calculating poll taxes</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>tax roll, tax register</li></ol>
